SELECT [p].[PersonIDN], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[CreationDate], [p].[IsDeleted], [p].[UpdatedBy], [p].[Modification_Date], [p].[PersonArabicName], [p].[PersonCode], [p].[PersonEnglishName], [p].[PersonIDC], [p].[PersonShortName], [p].[PersonStatus], [p].[Private], [p].[Website]
FROM [Persons] AS [p]
WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
